policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/ConfigMap/lgtm-loki-stack-test:
apiVersion: v1
data:
  test.sh: |
    #!/usr/bin/env bash

    LOKI_URI="http://${LOKI_SERVICE}:${LOKI_PORT}"

    function setup() {
      apk add -u curl jq
      until (curl -s ${LOKI_URI}/loki/api/v1/label/app/values | jq -e '.data[] | select(. == "loki")'); do
        sleep 1
      done
    }

    @test "Has labels" {
      curl -s ${LOKI_URI}/loki/api/v1/labels | \
      jq -e '.data[] | select(. == "app")'
    }

    @test "Query log entry" {
      curl -sG ${LOKI_URI}/api/prom/query?limit=10 --data-urlencode 'query={app="loki"}' | \
      jq -e '.streams[].entries | length >=1'
    }

    @test "Push log entry" {
      local timestamp=$(date +%!s(MISSING)000000000)
      local data=$(jq -n --arg timestamp "${timestamp}" '{"streams": [{"stream": {"app": "loki-test"}, "values": [[$timestamp, "foobar"]]}]}')

      curl -s -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" ${LOKI_URI}/loki/api/v1/push --data-raw "${data}"

      curl -sG ${LOKI_URI}/loki/api/v1/query_range?limit=1 --data-urlencode 'query={app="loki-test"}' | \
      jq -e '.data.result[].values[][1] == "foobar"'
    }
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  labels:
    app: loki-stack
    chart: loki-stack-2.10.2
    heritage: Helm
    release: lgtm
  name: lgtm-loki-stack-test
  namespace: default

---

##### FILE: librechat-deployment.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/librechat:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: librechat
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  revisionHistoryLimit: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: librechat
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: librechat
    spec:
      affinity:
        nodeAffinity:
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
            nodeSelectorTerms:
            - matchExpressions:
              - key: kubernetes.azure.com/role
                operator: In
                values:
                - agent
      containers:
      - envFrom:
        - configMapRef:
            name: librechat-configenv
        - secretRef:
            name: librechat-secrets
        image: ghcr.io/danny-avila/librechat:latest
        name: librechat
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3080
        resources:
          limits:
            cpu: "2"
            memory: 6Gi
          requests:
            cpu: "2"
            memory: 4Gi
        securityContext:
          runAsGroup: 3000
          runAsUser: 1000
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/librechat.yaml
          name: config-yaml
          readOnly: true
          subPath: librechat.yaml
        - mountPath: /app/client/public/images
          name: image-volume
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - sh
        - -c
        - chown -R 1000:3000 /app/client/public/images
        image: alpine:3
        name: take-data-dir-ownership
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/client/public/images
          name: image-volume
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: librechat-config
        name: config-yaml
      - name: image-volume
        persistentVolumeClaim:
          claimName: librechat-images-pvc

---

##### FILE: lifecycle1.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/lifecycle:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: lifecycle
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: lifecycle
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: lifecycle
    spec:
      containers:
      - command:
        - sh
        - -c
        - 'echo $(date +%!s(MISSING)): Running >> /timing && echo "The app is running!" && /bin/sleep
          120'
        image: busybox
        lifecycle:
          postStart:
            exec:
              command:
              - sh
              - -c
              - 'echo $(date +%!s(MISSING)): postStart >> /timing && sleep 10 && echo $(date
                +%!s(MISSING)): end postStart >> /timing'
          preStop:
            exec:
              command:
              - sh
              - -c
              - 'echo $(date +%!s(MISSING)): preStop >> /timing && sleep 10'
        livenessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - sh
            - -c
            - 'echo $(date +%!s(MISSING)): livenessProbe >> /timing'
          initialDelaySeconds: 35
          timeoutSeconds: 30
        name: lifecycle-container
        readinessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - sh
            - -c
            - 'echo $(date +%!s(MISSING)): readinessProbe >> /timing'
          initialDelaySeconds: 35
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - sh
        - -c
        - sleep 10
        image: busybox
        name: init

---

    meta.helm.sh/release-name: lighthouse
  labels:
    app: jenkins-x-lighthouse-gcjobs
    gitops.jenkins-x.io/pipeline: namespaces

  failedJobsHistoryLimit: 1
  jobTemplate:

      backoffLimit: 6
      template:
        metadata:
          labels:
            app: lighthouse-gc-jobs
            release: lighthouse
        spec:
          containers:
          - args:
            - --namespace=jx
            - --max-age=168h
            command:
            - /home/jx/gc-jobs
            env:
            - name: LOG_LEVEL
              value: info
            image: ghcr.io/jenkins-x/lighthouse-gc-jobs:1.14.4
            imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
            name: lighthouse-gc-jobs
            resources: {}
            terminationMessagePath: /dev/termination-log
            terminationMessagePolicy: File
          dnsPolicy: ClusterFirst
          restartPolicy: Never
          schedulerName: default-scheduler
          securityContext: {}
          serviceAccountName: lighthouse-gc-jobs
          terminationGracePeriodSeconds: 30
  schedule: 0/30 * * * *
  startingDeadlineSeconds: 4000
  successfulJobsHistoryLimit: 3
  suspend: false
